
  List of opcodes

From GTAMods Wiki
Jump to navigation <#mw-head> Jump to search <#p-search>

This is a list of all opcodes, including nops <https://gtamods.com/wiki/
List_of_unused_opcodes> and unsupported ones <https://gtamods.com/wiki/
List_of_unsupported_opcodes>, in GTA III <https://gtamods.com/wiki/
GTA_III>, Vice City <https://gtamods.com/wiki/Vice_City>, and San
Andreas <https://gtamods.com/wiki/San_Andreas>. Brief descriptions and
notes are added to the list for quick and easy access to information.

	5 	flt, flt, flt, flt, var 	get angle between 2D vectors 	
05A5 <https://gtamods.com/mediawiki/index.php?
title=05A5&action=edit&redlink=1> 	Vice City <https://gtamods.com/wiki/
Category:GTA_VC> San Andreas <https://gtamods.com/wiki/Category:GTA_SA>
	8 	flt, flt, flt, flt, flt, flt, flt, flt 	do 2d rectangles collide 	
05A6 <https://gtamods.com/mediawiki/index.php?
title=05A6&action=edit&redlink=1> 	Vice City <https://gtamods.com/wiki/
Category:GTA_VC> San Andreas <https://gtamods.com/wiki/Category:GTA_SA>
	4 	object handle, var, var, var 	get object rotation velocity 	
05A7 <https://gtamods.com/mediawiki/index.php?
title=05A7&action=edit&redlink=1> 	Vice City <https://gtamods.com/wiki/
Category:GTA_VC> San Andreas <https://gtamods.com/wiki/Category:GTA_SA>
	4 	object handle, var, var, var 	add velocity relative to object velocity 	
05A8 <https://gtamods.com/mediawiki/index.php?
title=05A8&action=edit&redlink=1> 	Vice City <https://gtamods.com/wiki/
Category:GTA_VC> San Andreas <https://gtamods.com/wiki/Category:GTA_SA>
	2 	object handle, var 	get object speed 	last opcode available for Vice
City PC

Some abbreviations and phrases used in this list:

int
    integer value
flt
    floating-point value
var
    variable to store a value or handle, either global or local unless
    specified
char
    character including actor and ped, apart from the player and special
    actor
car
    vehicle including car, bike, helicopter, plane, etc. unless specified
parameters rearranged...
    opcodes' parameters were rearranged from their original order mainly
    for sake of readability
restored in...
    opcode has been correctly or mostly simulated to work through the
    Opcodes Restoration Project <https://gtamods.com/wiki/
    Opcodes_Restoration_Project> plugin
used in...
    opcode has been used for the specified mod

<http://www.gtaforums.com/index.php?showtopic=217910>
